  var isDebugPage = window.location.href.match(/\/debug\/set-speedtrap\/index.html$/);
  var isPreviewPage = window.location.hostname.search(/^.*preview.*$/) !== -1;
  if (isDebugPage || isPreviewPage) return;
  var serviceWorkersSupported = !data.serviceWorkerCheck || 'serviceWorker' in navigator;
  var screenWidth = window.innerWidth;
  var viewportTooLarge = screenWidth >= data.width;

  var getCookieValue = function getCookieValue(name) {
    var matches = document.cookie.match(new RegExp("(^|;)\\s*".concat(name, "\\s*=\\s*([^;]+)")));

    if (matches) {
      return matches.pop();
    }

    return null;
  };

  var cookieValue = getCookieValue(data.cookie.name);
  var noCookieOrExceedsThreshold = !cookieValue || parseInt(cookieValue, 10) >= data.cookie.redirCutoffValue;
  var dtCookieValue = getCookieValue(data.dtCookie.name);
  var dtNoCookieOrExceedsThreshold = !dtCookieValue || parseInt(dtCookieValue, 10) >= data.dtCookie.redirCutoffValue;

  var findMatch = function findMatch(hosts) {
    return hosts.find(function (_ref) {
      var host = _ref.host;
      return window.location.hostname === host;
    });
  };

  var redirReplace = function redirReplace(redirBlockParam) {
    var match = findMatch(data.hosts);

    if (match && match.dest) {
      return window.location.replace("//".concat(match.dest).concat(window.location.pathname, "?").concat(redirBlockParam, "=").concat(Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000)));
    }

    return null;
  };

  if (viewportTooLarge) {
    // if in a larger viewport, check to see if user has the desktop/tablet cookie. if not, redirect them to michonne
    if (dtNoCookieOrExceedsThreshold) {
      var redirBlockParam = data.dtCookie.redirBlockParam;
      redirReplace(redirBlockParam);
    } // if in a smaller viewport, check to see if user has the mobile cookie. if not, redirect them to michonne

  } else if (!serviceWorkersSupported || noCookieOrExceedsThreshold) {
    var _redirBlockParam = data.cookie.redirBlockParam;
    redirReplace(_redirBlockParam);
  }

_9db439e9 speakable"><b data-type="sourceText">Hong Kong <!-- -->(CNN)<!-- --> —<!-- --> </b><span>China's top Hong Kong policy office will on Monday address the escalating protests in the semi-autonomous city over the past eight weekends. </span></div><div class="body-text_BodyText__UjdHO _9db439e9 speakable">The unrest reached fever pitch <a href="https://www.cnn.com/asia/live-news/hong-kong-central-protests-intl-hnk/index.html" target="_blank">Sunday</a> when riot police fired tear gas and rubber bullets at protesters as the two groups fought pitched battles in residential areas. It was the <a href="https://www.cnn.com/asia/live-news/hong-kong-yuen-long-protests-intl-hnk/index.html" target="_blank">second day of protests in a row </a>amid the deepening political crisis that shows few signs of deescalating.</div><div class="body-text_BodyText__UjdHO _9db439e9 speakable">Beijing's office dealing with Hong Kong and Macau affairs will give its first briefing on the issue from the Chinese capital at 3 p.m. local time Monday.</div><div class="_53039000"><div id="ad_rect_atf_02" class="ad-ad_rect_atf_02 _146ce769 _18afb79b"></div></div><div class="body-text_BodyText__UjdHO _9db439e9">On Sunday, protesters defied police orders to march through the center of the city, with groups splintering in different directions and blocking major roads. Many wore black, the adopted color of the protest movement, and carried signs condemning alleged police brutality. </div><div class="body-text_BodyText__UjdHO _9db439e9">Riot police confronted hundreds of mainly young protesters who tried to reach the Chinese government's Liaison Office. During demonstrations last weekend, activists vandalized the building and flung paint at the national emblem, drawing a furious reaction from Beijing. </div><div class="read-more-button"><div class="_53039000 e2048ec6"><button aria-label="" class="_1acd87bf" aria-disabled="false" href="" target="" type="">Read more</button></div></div><div class="componentOffScreen"><div class="_53039000 e9dfafb8"></div></div><div class="componentHidden"></div></div><div><div class="_53039000"><div class="c93b5e1d"><div class="OUTBRAIN" data-src="edition.cnn.com/2019/07/28/asia/hong-kong-protests-july-28-intl-hnk/index.html" data-widget-id="MB_13" data-ob-template="cnn"></div></div></div><div class="_53039000"></div><div class="_53039000"></div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div><div class="_53039000"><div class="PartnerZone"><div></div></div><div id="ad_bnr_btf_01" class="ad-ad_bnr_btf_01 _146ce769 _18afb79b"></div></div></div></div><div id="ad_nat_btf_01" class="ad-ad_nat_btf_01 _146ce769 _18afb79b _3b5323b0 _0e65240c"></div><div><div></div></div></div><noscript><p>Please enable JavaScript for a better experience.</p></noscript><script type="text/javascript" src="/js/manifest_17b60f34.js"></script><script type="text/javascript" src="/js/vendor_17b60f34.js"></script><script type="text/javascript" src="/js/main_17b60f34.js"></script><script src="//registry.api.cnn.io/bundles/fave/latest-2.x/js" id="script-FAVE" async="" defer=""></script></body></html>
